Bush’s was 57 percent, <a href="//www.cnn.com/2017/02/03/politics/donald-trump-approval-rating/">according to CNN</a>. Ronald Reagan was the closest to Trump, at 51 percent.</p><p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="The lowest current numbers have Trump at 35 approval (&lt;a href=&quot;//www.monmouth.edu/polling-institute/reports/MonmouthPoll_US_011717/&quot;&gt;Monmouth&lt;/a&gt;) and the highest at 52 percent (&lt;a href=&quot;//www.rasmussenreports.com/public_content/politics/trump_administration/january_2017/52_view_trump_favorably&quot;&gt;Rasmussen Reports&lt;/a&gt;)." data-reactid="18">The lowest current numbers have Trump at 35 approval (<a href="//www.monmouth.edu/polling-institute/reports/MonmouthPoll_US_011717/">Monmouth</a>) and the highest at 52 percent (<a href="//www.rasmussenreports.com/public_content/politics/trump_administration/january_2017/52_view_trump_favorably">Rasmussen Reports</a>).</p><p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="Looking at the statistics by race and gender, Trump’s&amp;nbsp;highest approval rating comes from white men. According to a &lt;a href=&quot;//twitter.com/epicciuto/status/835100439280508928&quot;&gt;NBC/SurveyMonkey poll&lt;/a&gt;, 58 percent of white men approve of Trump, while&amp;nbsp;just 14 percent of black women approve of him." data-reactid="19">Looking at the statistics by race and gender, Trump’s&nbsp;highest approval rating comes from white men. According to a <a href="//twitter.com/epicciuto/status/835100439280508928">NBC/SurveyMonkey poll</a>, 58 percent of white men approve of Trump, while&nbsp;just 14 percent of black women approve of him.</p><p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="&lt;b&gt;On feelings about Trump&lt;/b&gt;" data-reactid="20"><b>On feelings about Trump</b></p><p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="Another &lt;a href=&quot;//thehill.com/homenews/administration/320922-poll-trump-gets-41-percent-job-approval-rating&quot;&gt;McClatchy-Marist poll&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;says that 58 percent of Americans are embarrassed by the Trump administration, while 33 percent say his activity in office makes them proud." data-reactid="21">Another <a href="//thehill.com/homenews/administration/320922-poll-trump-gets-41-percent-job-approval-rating">McClatchy-Marist poll</a>&nbsp;says that 58 percent of Americans are embarrassed by the Trump administration, while 33 percent say his activity in office makes them proud.</p><p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="Naturally,&amp;nbsp;there’s a sharp contrast in Trump’s approval ratings between Democrats and Republicans. Though 85 percent of Republicans have a positive opinion of Trump, just 11 percent of Democrats do. This is a change from previous administrations, where the opposing party has had a higher approval rate of a president in the weeks after an inauguration. In the weeks after Obama’s inauguration, his approval rating was as high as 41 percent, &lt;a href=&quot;//www.gallup.com/poll/117355/obama-approval-rating-stable-polarized.aspx&quot;&gt;according to Gallup&lt;/a&gt;." data-reactid="22">Naturally,&nbsp;there’s a sharp contrast in Trump’s approval ratings between Democrats and Republicans. Though 85 percent of Republicans have a positive opinion of Trump, just 11 percent of Democrats do. This is a change from previous administrations, where the opposing party has had a higher approval rate of a president in the weeks after an inauguration. In the weeks after Obama’s inauguration, his approval rating was as high as 41 percent, <a href="//www.gallup.com/poll/117355/obama-approval-rating-stable-polarized.aspx">according to Gallup</a>.</p><p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="Thus far,&amp;nbsp;57 percent of people surveyed think Trump is attempting to do too much too quickly. But to that point, 75 percent do believe that Trump is staying true to the promises he made on the campaign trail.</p><p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="&lt;b&gt;On policy&lt;/b&gt;" data-reactid="24"><b>On policy</b></p><p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="As for Trump’s more controversial actions as president, 6 in 10 oppose the building of Trump’s much-talked about wall along the Mexican border, with 37 percent in support, &lt;a href=&quot;//thehill.com/homenews/administration/320845-poll-voters-opposed-to-several-proposals-by-trump-gop&quot;&gt;according to a Quinnipiac poll&lt;/a&gt;." data-reactid="25">As for Trump’s more controversial actions as president, 6 in 10 oppose the building of Trump’s much-talked about wall along the Mexican border, with 37 percent in support, <a href="//thehill.com/homenews/administration/320845-poll-voters-opposed-to-several-proposals-by-trump-gop">according to a Quinnipiac poll</a>.</p><p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="People are split a bit more evenly on healthcare, the same poll reports: 54 percent oppose repealing Obamacare, or the Affordable Care Act, and 43 support its repeal. One in three voters are either “very” or “somewhat” concerned about losing their healthcare if Congressional Republicans (and Trump) follow through on their vow to overturn Obamacare." data-reactid="26">People are split a bit more evenly on healthcare, the same poll reports: 54 percent oppose repealing Obamacare, or the Affordable Care Act, and 43 support its repeal. One in three voters are either “very” or “somewhat” concerned about losing their healthcare if Congressional Republicans (and Trump) follow through on their vow to overturn Obamacare.</p><p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="About &lt;a href=&quot;//thehill.com/homenews/administration/320845-poll-voters-opposed-to-several-proposals-by-trump-gop&quot;&gt;three-quarters of those surveyed&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;do not want to lower taxes for the wealthy." data-reactid="27">About <a href="//thehill.com/homenews/administration/320845-poll-voters-opposed-to-several-proposals-by-trump-gop">three-quarters of those surveyed</a>&nbsp;do not want to lower taxes for the wealthy.</p><p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="In nearly every poll, a majority of respondents say the country is not heading in the right direction. In a Monmouth poll, just 27 percent of people support the way the country is headed — and 67 percent don’t approve of the direction the country is heading. Rasmussen Reports, &lt;a href=&quot;//content.time.com/time/magazine/article/0,9171,1946935,00.html&quot;&gt;a conservative-leaning poll group&lt;/a&gt;, according to &lt;em&gt;Time&lt;/em&gt;, currently has&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;//www.realclearpolitics.com/epolls/other/direction_of_country-902.html&quot;&gt;46 percent approval and 48 percent disapproval&lt;/a&gt;." data-reactid="28">In nearly every poll, a majority of respondents say the country is not heading in the right direction. In a Monmouth poll, just 27 percent of people support the way the country is headed — and 67 percent don’t approve of the direction the country is heading. Rasmussen Reports, <a href="//content.time.com/time/magazine/article/0,9171,1946935,00.html">a conservative-leaning poll group</a>, according to <em>Time</em>, currently has&nbsp;<a href="//www.realclearpolitics.com/epolls/other/direction_of_country-902.html">46 percent approval and 48 percent disapproval</a>.</p><p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="On Trump’s controversial travel ban, which has since been blocked by a federal judge and later, an appellate court, 48 percent do consider it to be a “Muslim ban,” and 65 percent of people oppose it." data-reactid="29">On Trump’s controversial travel ban, which has since been blocked by a federal judge and later, an appellate court, 48 percent do consider it to be a “Muslim ban,” and 65 percent of people oppose it.</p><p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="&lt;a href=&quot;//www.publicpolicypolling.com/main/2017/02/americans-now-evenly-divided-on-impeaching-trump.html&quot;&gt;45 percent of respondents&lt;/a&gt; support Trump’s executive orders on immigration. However, among that 45 percent, 51 percent of them think the fictional Bowling Green Massacre is evidence for a need in Trump’s new immigration policy." data-reactid="30"><a href="//www.publicpolicypolling.com/main/2017/02/americans-now-evenly-divided-on-impeaching-trump.html">45 percent of respondents</a> support Trump’s executive orders on immigration. about Russian President Vladimir Putin." data-reactid="31"><a href="//www.publicpolicypolling.com/main/2017/02/americans-now-evenly-divided-on-impeaching-trump.html">72 percent of people do not approve of Trump’s favorable comments</a> about Russian President Vladimir Putin.</p><p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="It’s a near even split on how people view Trump is dealing with the economy: &lt;a href=&quot;//thehill.com/homenews/administration/320922-poll-trump-gets-41-percent-job-approval-rating&quot;&gt;45 percent approve, while 43 percent disapprove&lt;/a&gt;." data-reactid="32">It’s a near even split on how people view Trump is dealing with the economy: <a href="//thehill.com/homenews/administration/320922-poll-trump-gets-41-percent-job-approval-rating">45 percent approve, while 43 percent disapprove</a>.</p><p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="&lt;strong&gt;RELATED VIDEO: Watch: Natasha Stoynoff Breaks Silence, Accuses Donald Trump of Sexual Attack&lt;/strong&gt;" data-reactid="33"><strong>RELATED VIDEO: Watch: Natasha Stoynoff Breaks Silence, Accuses Donald Trump of Sexual Attack</strong></p><p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="&lt;b&gt;On other topics and events&lt;/b&gt;" data-reactid="34"><b>On other topics and events</b></p><p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="Trump made headlines for his comments about Frederick Douglass a few weeks ago, and according to a Public Policy Polling poll, only 47 percent of Trump voters know who Douglass is.
